      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses that will occur in the 25th century
       </b>
       . During the period 2401 to 2500 there will be 237
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 81 will be partial, 89 will be annular (two
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Terminology" title="Solar eclipse">
        non-central
       </a>
       ), 66 will be total (one non-central), and 1 will be hybrid. The greatest number of eclipses in one year will be four, occurring in 7 different years: 2416, 2434, 2452, 2456, 2474, 2485 and 2492.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
